Now I understand the diagnostics manager. I can see that:\n\n1. The `DiagnosticsManager` class manages diagnostics for files in a `ResourceMap<FileDiagnostics>`\n2. It has a `_currentDiagnostics` field that is a `vscode.DiagnosticCollection` which is the actual collection displayed in the Problems panel\n3. Now I have a good understanding of the issue. The BufferSyncSupport class:\n\n1. Manages synced buffers (open files)\n2. Listens to `onDidChangeTextDocument` events (line 520)\n3. Listens to `onDidOpenTextDocument` and `onDidCloseTextDocument` events\n4. Requests diagnostics through `requestDiagnostic` method\n\nThe issue is that when Git switches branches and files on disk change, the buffer sync support doesn't detect these changes because:\n- The text document itself hasn't changed in the editor\n- File system changes don't trigger text document change events\n- Diagnostics remain stale because they were cached for the old file content\n\nThe {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01FgJrWMmWVMZonVJbeFSXHg","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01VHJyRbwXkg623MsRTY8JAU","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/IMPLEMENTATION_GUIDE.md","content":"# VS Code Stale Diagnostics Fix - Implementation Guide\n\n## Problem Statement\n\nUsers experience stale TypeScript diagnostics in the Problems panel after switching Git branches. Files that no longer have errors still display old errors from the previous branch until the user manually opens and edits each file.\n\n### Root Cause\n\nThe TypeScript diagnostics pipeline only refreshes when text content changes in the editor (`onDidChangeTextDocument` events). File-on-disk changes from Git operations are not detected, leaving diagnostics stale until the user triggers an edit.\n\n## Solution Architecture\n\nThe fix adds file system change detection to the `BufferSyncSupport` class, which manages the synchronization of open file buffers with the TypeScript server.\n\n### Key Changes\n\n**File**: `extensions/typescript-language-features/src/tsServer/bufferSyncSupport.ts`\n\n#### 1. **listen() Method Enhancement** (Line 530-531)\nAdd file system watcher setup during initialization:\n```typescript\n// Watch for file system changes (e.g., from git operations) to detect stale diagnostics\nthis.setupFileSystemWatcher();\n```\n\n#### 2. **setupFileSystemWatcher() Method** (New)\nCreates watchers for TypeScript/JavaScript files and registers listeners:\n- Pattern: `**/*.ts`, `**/*.tsx`, `**/*.js`, `**/*.jsx`\n- On file change: Triggers diagnostic refresh\n- On file delete: Clears stale diagnostics\n- Watchers are registered for disposal with `this._disposables`\n\n#### 3. **onFileSystemChange() Handler** (New)\nHandles file modification events from disk:\n- For synced buffers: Calls `requestDiagnostic()` to refresh\n- For non-synced files: Triggers diagnostic request if it's a TS/JS file\n- Uses existing diagnostic pipeline for consistency\n\n#### 4. **onFileSystemDelete() Handler** (New)\nHandles file deletion events:\n- Removes pending diagnostics for the deleted file\n- Clears the file from any in-flight diagnostic requests\n- Prevents \"ghost\" error messages for deleted files\n\n#### 5. **shouldTriggerDiagnosticsForFile() Helper** (New)\nValidates that a file is a TypeScript/JavaScript file before triggering diagnostics:\n- Returns `true` for: `.ts`, `.tsx`, `.js`, `.jsx`\n- Prevents unnecessary diagnostic requests for other file types\n\n## Flow Diagram\n\n```\nGit Branch Switch\n    ↓\nFiles change on disk\n    ↓\nFileSystemWatcher detects change\n    ↓\nonFileSystemChange() called\n    ↓\nrequestDiagnostic() or pendingDiagnostics.set()\n    ↓\ntriggerDiagnostics() schedules refresh\n    ↓\nsendPendingDiagnostics() runs GetErrRequest\n    ↓\nTypeScript Server re-analyzes files\n    ↓\nUpdated diagnostics displayed in Problems panel\n```\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Watcher Registration Pattern\n```typescript\nconst watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(pattern);\nwatcher.onDidChange((uri) => this.onFileSystemChange(uri), this, this._disposables);\nwatcher.onDidDelete((uri) => this.onFileSystemDelete(uri), this, this._disposables);\nthis._disposables.push(watcher);\n```\n\nThis pattern ensures:\n- Event handlers have proper `this` context\n- Watchers are automatically disposed when `BufferSyncSupport` is disposed\n- Consistent lifecycle management with existing code\n\n### Diagnostic Update Mechanism\nThe solution reuses existing methods rather than creating new ones:\n- `requestDiagnostic(buffer)` - For synced buffers\n- `pendingDiagnostics.set(uri, timestamp)` - For non-synced files\n- `triggerDiagnostics()` - Schedules the diagnostic update\n- `GetErrRequest.executeGetErrRequest()` - Fetches diagnostics from TypeScript server\n\nThis ensures compatibility with:\n- Project-wide diagnostics configuration\n- Region-based diagnostics\n- Existing debouncing and performance optimizations\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\n### Manual Testing\n1. Open a TypeScript/JavaScript file with errors\n2. Switch Git branch that removes/changes those errors\n3. Verify Problems panel updates without manual edits\n\n### Automated Testing\nCreate tests for:\n- File change event triggers diagnostic refresh\n- File delete clears pending diagnostics\n- Non-TS/JS files are ignored\n- Multiple file watchers don't cause duplicates\n- Watcher disposal on extension shutdown\n\n### Edge Cases\n- Files open in editor when branch changes\n- Files deleted on disk while open in editor\n- Rapid file changes (debouncing)\n- Projects with many TypeScript files\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n1. **File Watcher Cost**: Only watches `.ts`, `.tsx`, `.js`, `.jsx` files\n2. **Debouncing**: Uses existing `diagnosticDelayer` (300ms default)\n3. **Optimization**: Only synced buffers are actively validated\n4. **Deduplication**: Existing `pendingDiagnostics` prevents duplicate requests\n\n## Compatibility\n\n- **VS Code API**: Uses standard `vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher()`\n- **Extension Host**: No changes needed to communication protocol\n- **TypeScript Server**: Uses existing diagnostics requests (`geterr`, `geterrForProject`)\n- **Backward Compatibility**: No breaking changes to existing APIs\n\n## Applying the Fix\n\n### Option 1: Manual Application\nApply the patch file:\n```bash\ncd /workspace\ngit apply stale-diagnostics-fix.patch\n```\n\n### Option 2: Manual Edits\nFollow the line numbers in the patch file to make the changes manually.\n\n### Option 3: Using the Work File\nCopy the implementation from `/workspace/work/bufferSyncSupport.ts` to the source location.\n\n## Verification\n\nAfter applying the fix:\n\n1. **Compilation**: Should compile without errors\n   ```bash\n   npm run compile\n   ```\n\n2. **Type Checking**: TypeScript should validate without issues\n\n3. **Runtime Testing**:\n   - Create a test project with TypeScript errors\n   - Switch Git branches\n   - Verify diagnostics update automatically\n\n4. **Regression Testing**: Run existing test suite\n   ```bash\n   npm test\n   ```\n\n## Success Criteria\n\n✓ Stale diagnostics are cleared when files change on disk\n✓ New diagnostics appear after Git branch switch\n✓ Diagnostics refresh without requiring manual file edits\n✓ Problems panel reflects current state of files\n✓ No performance regression from additional file watchers\n✓ Code follows VS Code conventions and patterns\n✓ All tests pass\n\n## Related Code\n\n- **DiagnosticsManager**: `extensions/typescript-language-features/src/languageFeatures/diagnostics.ts`\n  - Manages the `DiagnosticCollection` displayed in the Problems panel\n\n- **TypeScriptServiceClient**: `extensions/typescript-language-features/src/typescriptServiceClient.ts`\n  - Creates and owns the `BufferSyncSupport` instance\n\n- **File Change Events**: VS Code API for file system watchers\n  - `vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher()`\n  - Events: `onDidChange`, `onDidDelete`, `onDidCreate`\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\n1. Monitor for file create events to add new files to diagnostics\n2. Add configuration option to disable file watching\n3. Implement exponential backoff for rapid file changes\n4. Track performance metrics for file watching operations\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":2,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1276,"cache_read_input_tokens":91680,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1276},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"da177922-02a3-4c6e-a098-3251b1aa1701","uuid":"8dd9255f-2ce7-47a1-a492-6f90af5d0f2e"}

Files that no longer have errors still display old errors from the previous branch until the user manually opens and edits each file.\n\n### Root Cause\n\nThe TypeScript diagnostics pipeline only refreshes when text content changes in the editor (`onDidChangeTextDocument` events). File-on-disk changes from Git operations are not detected, leaving diagnostics stale until the user triggers an edit.\n\n## Solution Architecture\n\nThe fix adds file system change detection to the `BufferSyncSupport` class, which manages the synchronization of open file buffers with the TypeScript server.\n\n### Key Changes\n\n**File**: `extensions/typescript-language-features/src/tsServer/bufferSyncSupport.ts`\n\n#### 1. **listen() Method Enhancement** (Line 530-531)\nAdd file system watcher setup during initialization:\n```typescript\n// Watch for file system changes (e.g., from git operations) to detect stale diagnostics\nthis.setupFileSystemWatcher();\n```\n\n#### 2. **setupFileSystemWatcher() For synced buffers: Calls `requestDiagnostic()` to refresh\n- For non-synced files: Triggers diagnostic request if it's a TS/JS file\n- Uses existing diagnostic pipeline for consistency\n\n#### 4. **onFileSystemDelete() Handler** (New)\nHandles file deletion events:\n- Removes pending diagnostics for the deleted file\n- Clears the file from any in-flight diagnostic requests\n- Prevents \"ghost\" error messages for deleted files\n\n#### 5. **shouldTriggerDiagnosticsForFile() Helper** (New)\nValidates that a file is a TypeScript/JavaScript file before triggering diagnostics:\n- Returns `true` for: `.ts`, `.tsx`, `.js`, `.jsx`\n- Prevents unnecessary diagnostic requests for other file types\n\n## Flow Diagram\n\n```\nGit Branch Switch\n    ↓\nFiles change on disk\n    ↓\nFileSystemWatcher detects change\n    ↓\nonFileSystemChange() called\n    ↓\nrequestDiagnostic() or pendingDiagnostics.set()\n    ↓\ntriggerDiagnostics() schedules refresh\n    ↓\nsendPendingDiagnostics() runs GetErrRequest\n    ↓\nTypeScript Server re-analyzes files\n    ↓\nUpdated diagnostics displayed in Problems panel\n```\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Watcher Registration Pattern\n```typescript\nconst watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(pattern);\nwatcher.onDidChange((uri) => this.onFileSystemChange(uri), this, this._disposables);\nwatcher.onDidDelete((uri) => this.onFileSystemDelete(uri), this, this._disposables);\nthis._disposables.push(watcher);\n```\n\nThis pattern ensures:\n- Event handlers have proper `this` context\n- Watchers are automatically disposed when `BufferSyncSupport` is disposed\n- Consistent lifecycle management with existing code\n\n### Diagnostic Update Mechanism\nThe solution reuses existing methods rather than creating new ones:\n- `requestDiagnostic(buffer)` - For synced buffers\n- `pendingDiagnostics.set(uri, timestamp)` - For non-synced files\n- `triggerDiagnostics()` - Schedules the diagnostic update\n- `GetErrRequest.executeGetErrRequest()` - Fetches diagnostics from TypeScript server\n\nThis ensures compatibility with:\n- Project-wide diagnostics configuration\n- Region-based diagnostics\n- Existing debouncing and performance optimizations\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\n### Manual Testing\n1. Open a TypeScript/JavaScript file with errors\n2. Switch Git branch that removes/changes those errors\n3. Files on disk change (potentially resolving TypeScript errors)\n2. The editor's text buffer remains unchanged\n3. Diagnostics are not refreshed because they only update on `onDidChangeTextDocument` events\n4. Users see stale errors from the old branch until they manually edit each file\n\n## The Solution\n\nAdd file system watchers to the `BufferSyncSupport` class that:\n1. Detect when TypeScript/JavaScript files change on disk\n2. Trigger the existing diagnostic update pipeline\n3. Clear diagnostics for deleted files\n4. Maintain performance by reusing existing infrastructure\n\n## Architecture Overview\n\n### Current Flow\n```\nText Document Change\n    ↓\nonDidChangeTextDocument event\n    ↓\nrequestDiagnostic(buffer)\n    ↓\npendingDiagnostics.set()\n    ↓\ntriggerDiagnostics()\n    ↓\nGetErrRequest (TypeScript Server)\n    ↓\nProblems Panel Updated\n```\n\n### New Flow (Addition)\n```\nFile System Change (from Git)\n    ↓\nFileSystemWatcher event\n    ↓\nonFileSystemChange(uri)\n    ↓\nrequestDiagnostic(buffer) OR pendingDiagnostics.set()\n    ↓\n[continues through existing diagnostic pipeline...]\n```\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Four New Methods in BufferSyncSupport\n\n**1. `setupFileSystemWatcher()`**\n- Creates watchers for `**/*.ts`, `**/*.tsx`, `**/*.js`, `**/*.jsx`\n- Registers change and delete event handlers\n- Ensures proper cleanup via `this._disposables`\n\n**2. `onFileSystemChange(uri)`**\n- Handles file modification events\n- For open buffers: calls `requestDiagnostic()`\n- For closed files: queues them in `pendingDiagnostics`\n\n**3. `onFileSystemDelete(uri)`**\n- Clears pending diagnostics for deleted file\n- Prevents in-flight diagnostic requests from orphaned files\n\n**4. `shouldTriggerDiagnosticsForFile(uri)`**\n- Helper to validate file extension\n- Prevents unnecessary watchers on non-source files\n\n### Integration Point\n\nOne line added to `listen()` method:\n```typescript\nthis.setupFileSystemWatcher();\n```\n\nThis ensures file watchers are set up when the language service begins listening for changes.\n\n## Files Modified\n\n```\nextensions/typescript-language-features/src/tsServer/bufferSyncSupport.ts\n- Line ~530: Call to setupFileSystemWatcher()\n- Line ~770-835: Four new private methods\n```\n\n**Total Changes**: 60 new lines of code\n\n## Key Benefits\n\n1. **Automatic Refresh**: Diagnostics update automatically after branch switches\n2. **Consistent with Existing Code**: Uses same diagnostic update mechanisms\n3. **No Breaking Changes**: Only adds new functionality, doesn't modify existing APIs\n4. **Performance Optimized**:\n   - Reuses existing debouncing (300ms delay)\n   - Only watches TS/JS files\n   - Respects existing validation settings\n5. **Maintainable**: Clear separation of concerns with dedicated methods\n\n## Testing Approach\n\n### Unit Tests\n- Files that no longer have errors still show old errors until the user manually opens and edits each file.\r\n\r\n## Root Cause\r\nThe diagnostics pipeline only refreshes on in-editor text changes (onDidChangeTextDocument). File-on-disk changes from Git operations don't trigger diagnostic updates.\r\n\r\n## Key Components\r\n1. **DiagnosticsManager** - `/workspace/extensions/typescript-language-features/src/languageFeatures/diagnostics.ts`\r\n   - Manages `_currentDiagnostics` (vscode.DiagnosticCollection displayed in Problems panel)\r\n   - Methods: `updateDiagnostics()`, `deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile()`, `reInitialize()`\r\n\r\n2. **BufferSyncSupport** - `/workspace/extensions/typescript-language-features/src/tsServer/bufferSyncSupport.ts`\r\n   - Listens to `onDidChangeTextDocument` events (line 520)\r\n   - Manages synced buffers (open files)\r\n   - Triggers diagnostics through `requestDiagnostic()` -> `triggerDiagnostics()`\r\n\r\n3. **TypeScriptServiceClient** - Creates and uses DiagnosticsManager\r\n\r\n## Solution Approach\r\nAdd file system change detection in BufferSyncSupport:\r\n1. Watch for file changes using `vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher`\r\n2. On file change events, trigger diagnostic refresh for affected files\r\n3. On file delete events, clear diagnostics for those files\r\n"}}

in the class)\n\n### New Method 1: setupFileSystemWatcher()\n```typescript\nprivate setupFileSystemWatcher(): void {\n    // Create file system watchers for TypeScript and JavaScript files\n    const patterns = [\n        '**/*.ts',\n        '**/*.tsx',\n        '**/*.js',\n        '**/*.jsx',\n    ];\n\n    for (const pattern of patterns) {\n        const watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(pattern);\n\n        watcher.onDidChange((uri) => {\n            // File was modified on disk - refresh diagnostics for this file\n            this.onFileSystemChange(uri);\n        }, this, this._disposables);\n\n        watcher.onDidDelete((uri) => {\n            // File was deleted - clear diagnostics for this file\n            this.onFileSystemDelete(uri);\n        }, this, this._disposables);\n\n        this._disposables.push(watcher);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Purpose**: Creates file system watchers for all TypeScript and JavaScript files. Registers event handlers for file changes and deletions. Ensures proper cleanup via `this._disposables`.\n\n### New Method 2: onFileSystemChange()\n```typescript\nprivate onFileSystemChange(uri: vscode.Uri): void {\n    const syncedBuffer = this.syncedBuffers.get(uri);\n    if (syncedBuffer) {\n        // File has changed on disk, request fresh diagnostics\n        this.requestDiagnostic(syncedBuffer);\n    } else {\n        // File not currently synced, but request diagnostics anyway\n        // This handles cases where the file is open but hasn't been modified in the editor\n        if (this.shouldTriggerDiagnosticsForFile(uri)) {\n            this.pendingDiagnostics.set(uri, Date.now());\n            this.triggerDiagnostics();\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Purpose**: Handles file modification events from the file system watcher. For open buffers, calls `requestDiagnostic()`. For closed files, queues them in `pendingDiagnostics` for later processing.\n\n### New Method 3: onFileSystemDelete()\n```typescript\nprivate onFileSystemDelete(uri: vscode.Uri): void {\n    const syncedBuffer = this.syncedBuffers.get(uri);\n    if (syncedBuffer) {\n        // Clear diagnostics for deleted file\n        this.pendingDiagnostics.delete(uri);\n        this.pendingGetErr?.files.delete(uri);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Purpose**: Handles file deletion events. Removes any pending diagnostics for the deleted file and clears it from any in-flight diagnostic requests.\n\n### New Method 4: shouldTriggerDiagnosticsForFile()\n```typescript\nprivate shouldTriggerDiagnosticsForFile(uri: vscode.Uri): boolean {\n    // Only trigger diagnostics for TypeScript/JavaScript files\n    const fileName = uri.fsPath.toLowerCase();\n    return fileName.endsWith('.ts') || fileName.endsWith('.tsx') ||\n        fileName.endsWith('.js') || fileName.endsWith('.jsx');\n}\n```\n\n**Purpose**: Validates that a file is a TypeScript or JavaScript file before triggering diagnostics. Prevents unnecessary diagnostic requests for other file types.\n\n## Summary of Changes\n\n| Metric | Before | After | Change |\n|--------|--------|-------|--------|\n| Total Lines | 773 | 834 | +61
